<rating>5< /rating>< Review>
When I bought my house, inspections revealed that the sewer line from the sidewalk to the city connection was old and cracked. Also, a section of sewer line in the crawlspace under the house was clay pipe, which is the wrong kind of pipe.

I called a few plumbers; Flood Brothers was by far the most professional in their response. Michael came out, looked things over and told me that I didn't have to pay to replace the cracked sewer line yet, as it still had some lifespan left in it. He recommended adding a cleanout for easy access in the future. Great idea!

He hydrojetted the sewer line, added the cleanout, and replaced the clay pipe under my house. I was out of town during the work, and his communication was excellent: he was conscientious in keeping me informed about the status of the job.

In a year, he will come back and send a camera down the line at no cost to me, to see if it's still holding up. Fantastic that Flood Brothers stand by their work!

I'd recommend Flood Brothers for sure. They're on my list for the next big job, installing a tankless water heater...< /Review>

I always enjoy going to this doctors office. Dr. Azizzadeh is informative and really good at what he does. At this doctors office, I've been through it all.
